\bentry
\word[U(1)]{U}
\pron{yU}
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{Us} yA \eng{U's} )}
\bmng
(\eng{u} eMdU \parx) 
\bnum
\num{1}iMgilxSf vaNRmAleya ipapxtotxMdaneya akaSxra. 
\num{2} \eng{U} AkArada vasutx yA vakarx(reVKe) (\kanmu\ \saMpa gaLalilx baLake): \eng{U-bolt.} 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[U(2)]{U} 
\pron{U} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
(bamIRyaralilx) obabxna hesarina muMde seVrisuva gwravasUcaka birudu. 
\emng
\eentry

\num{2} meVluvagaRda vishiSaTx lkaSxN eMdu naMbalAda. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry

\pron{yU} 
\gl{\saMkiSx}

\pron{yUbikivxTi} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng

\emng

\expl{}
\bmng

\expl{}
\bmng

\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[unbound(1)]{unbound} 
\pron{anfbwMDf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} baMdhana kaLeda; kaTuTx harida. 
\num{2} anibaRMdhita. 
\numi{3} (pusatxkada \vi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} pusatxkarUpavAgi kaTTxda; biDihALegaLiruva; raTuTx hAkillxda. 
\alnum{b} kAgadada hodikeyiruva. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{4} (darxvayx yA kaNda \vi) biDiyAgiruva; saMyukatxvAgirada yA baMdhitavAgillxda. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bnum

\num{2} (\AmA) arivaLida sithxtiyalilx; parxjAcnxhiVna avasethxyalilx: \eng{put him under for the operation} shasatxrXcikitesxgAgi avananunx arivaLikeya sithxtiyalilxDu. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_b.pdf}{B}{bring nuga(26)}{bring} under .} 
\num{2} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_k.pdf}{K}{keep(1) nuga(37)}{${}^1$keep} under .} 
\num{3} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_k.pdf}{K}{knuckle(2) pagu(1)}{${}^2$knuckle} under .} 
\num{4} \eng{the ship went under} haDagu muLugitu. 
\num{5} \eng{can you stay under (the water) for 2 hours} niVnu niVrinaDiyalilx eraDu gaMTe irabalelxyA? 
\enum
\emng

\bnum
\num{1} BUmiya keLage; neldaDiyalilx: \eng{miners working underground} BUmiya keLage, neldaDi -- kelsa mADutitxruva gaNi kelsagAraru. 
\num{2} guTATxgi; goVpayxdalilx; rahasayxvAgi: \eng{go underground} bacicxTuTxko; mareyAgu; kANdAgu. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word[underground(2)]{underground} 
\pron{aMDarfgwrxMDf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} BUmiya keLagiruva; neldoLagiruva. 
\num{2} goVpayxvAda; rahasayxda; guTATxda; mareyalilxna; (\kanmu\ ALutitxruva parxButavxvanunx bauDameVlu mADalu) rahasayxvAgi kelsa mADuva: \eng{underground movement} rahasayx caLuvaLi. 
\num{3} asAMparxdAyika; pArxyoVgikavAda: \eng{underground press} pArxyoVgika mudarxNAlya. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
 \eng{underground workers} rahasayx caLuvaLiya sadasayxru. 
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{understand} 
\pron{aMDarfsATxYxMDf}
\gl{\kirx}
\expl{(\BU\ matutx \BUkaq\ \eng{understood} \ucAcx-- aMDarfsuTxDf). }


\noindent
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (mAtugaLu, vayxkitx, BASe, \mo vugaLa) athaR -- garxhisu, hiDi; athaRmADiko; ari(tuko); tiLi(duko): \eng{does not understand what you say} niVnu heVLuvudu(avanige) athaRvAguvudillx. \eng{understands you perfectly} ninanxnunx pUNRvAgi aritukoMDidAdxne. \eng{cannot understand French} pherxMcfBASeyanunx athaRmADikoLaLxlAra. 
\num{2} (udedxVsha, vivaraNe yA kAraNvanunx) garxhisu; ari; tiLi; Uhisu; gotutx mADiko; athaR mADiko: \eng{do not understand why he came} avanu yAke baMdanoV nanage tiLiyadu. \eng{could not understand what the noise was about} A galATe yAvudara bagegx eMbaudu gotAtxgalillx. \eng{do not understand the point of his remark} avana TiVkeya aMshavanunx nAnu athaRmADikoLaLxlAre. 
\num{3} (yAvudAdarU sUcane yA mAhitiya AdhArada meVle Uhe, tiVmARna, \mo vugaLige baruvalilx) naMbau; eNisu; Uhisu; BAvisu; takiRsu: \eng{I understand that it begins at noon} adu madhAyxhanx pArxraMBavAgutatxdeMdu nananx Uhe. \eng{I understand that expenses were to be paid} KcuRmADiruvudanunx tuMbikoDalAgutatxdeMdu nAnu eNisutetxVne. 
\num{4} (AshacxyaR, koVpa, saMdeVha, \mo vanunx sUcisuvAga) tiLi; garxhisu; aMduko: \eng{am I to understand that you refuse?} niVnu nirAkarisutitxVyeMdu tiLiyaleV? 
\num{5} (manasisxnalilx) (padavanunx) adhAyxhAra mADiko: \eng{the verb may be either expressed or understood} kirxyApada vAcayxvAgirabahudu yA adhAyxhAravAgirabahudu. 
\num{6} lkaSxN yA savxBAvavanunx sahAnuBUtiyiMda -- athaRmADiko, tiLi, gamanisu, aritiru: \eng{quite understand your difficulty} ninanx kaSaTx nanage athaRvAgutatxde (nAnu balelx). \eng{cannot understand him at all} avananunx athaRmADikoLuLxvudeV kaSaTx. 
\num{7}(heVge nivaRhisabeVkeMbaudanunx, vayxvaharisabeVkeMbaudanunx) aritiru; athaRmADikoMDiru: \eng{could never understand algebra} biVjgaNitavanunx eMdU athaRmADikoLaLxlAgiradavanAgidedx. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\akirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} (sAmAnayxvAgi yA vishiSaTx athaRdalilx) athaRvAgu; arivAgu. 
\num{2} (UheyiMda yA Kcita AdhArada meVle) tiLi; garxhisu; naMbau: \eng{he is coming to -- morrow, I understand} (avanu nALe barutAtxneMdu keVLide, hwde?) avanu nALe barutitxdAdxneMdu tiLididedxVne. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{\hyperref{kandict_g.pdf}{G}{give(1) pagu(16)}{${}^1$give} person to understand .} 
\num{2} \eng{tongue not understanded of the people} (\pArxparx) jnakekx athaRvAgadidadx paricayavillxdidadx BASe, anayxBASe, paraBASe. 
\numi{3} \eng{understand each other} 
\banum
\alnum{a} obabxrigobabxru athaRmADikoLiLx; parasapxrara aBipArxya, BAvane, \mo vanunx garxhisikoLiLx. 
\alnum{b} parasapxra omamxtadalilxri yA oLasaMcinalilx BAgigaLAgiri. 
\eanum
\numie
\enum
\emng

\bentry

\pron{yUnilAYxTra(rf)lf} 
\gl{\gu}
\expl{}
\bmng

\num{2} oMdeV pakaSx yA vayxkitxge saMbaMdhisida; oMdeV pakaSx yA vayxkitx keYkoMDa: \eng{unilateral declaration of independence} EkapakiSxVyavAda sAvxtaMtarxyX GoVSaNe. 
\num{3} (rasetxya badiyalilx vAhanAdigaLanunx nililxsuva \vi) rasetxya omamxgagxlige mAtarx niyamitavAda; oMdeV pakakxda. 
\num{4} (sasayxgaLa \vi) EkapAshaRvxka; EkapAshivxRVya; tALina oMdeV pakakxdiMda horaTiruva, oMdeV pakakxdalilxruva. 
\num{5} (saMtatiya vaMshAnukarxmada \vi) EkaliMgada; oMdeV liMgada pUviRkariMda baMda.

\bentry
\word{union} 
\pron{yUnayxnf, yUnianf} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} okakxTuTx; okUkxT; aikayx; seVrike; saMyoVga: \eng{the union of the parts was imperfect} BAgagaLa seVrike asamapaRkavAgitutx. 
\num{2} maduve; vivAha (saMbaMdha): \eng{a happy union} suKvAda vivAha saMbaMdha. 
\num{3} hoMdike; sAmarasayx; sAMgatayx; meYtirx; EkiVBAva: \eng{lived together in perfect union} saMpUNRvAda meYtirxyiMda oMdAgi jiVvana naDesidaru. 
\numi{4} (vividha BAgagaLu seVri racitavAgiruva) rAjkiVya okUkxT: 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\kanmu) amerikada saMyukatx saMsAthxnagaLu. 
\alnum{b} gerxVTf birxTnf matutx \kanu\ aileRMDu. 
\alnum{c} dakiSxN Aphirxkada okUkxT. 
\alnum{d} soVviyeTf okUkxT. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{5} (\ga) kUT; eraDu athavA hecucx gaN \eng{(set)} gaLige seVrida ellx dhAtugaLanUnx oLagoMDa motatx. 
\num{6} saMGa; saMGaTne; aMgaBAgagaLu yA sadasayxru parasapxra kUDi racitavAda okUkxTda vayxvasethx. 
\numi{7} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (\ca) pAyxriSf kUT; saMyukatx pAyxriSf; nigaRtikara jiVvanAdhAra kAnUnugaLa nivARhakAkxgi oMdugUDisida halvu pAyxriSfgaLu. 
\hypertarget{union(7)b}{} 
\alnum{b} iMtha saMyukatx pAyxriSf sAthxpisida UT-vasati odagisuva, nigaRtikara Alya; anAthAlya. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{8} (\birx) (sahakArakAkxgi) oMdugUDisida cacuRgaLa kUT. 
\numi{9} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (vishavxvidAyxnilyada yA kAleVjina) vidAyxthiR saMGa yA cacARsaMGa: \eng{the debate at the Oxford union} AkfsxphaDfR vidAyxthiRsaMGadalilx naDeda cacARkUT. 
\alnum{b} iMtha saMGada vasati kaTTxDagaLu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{10} gerxVTf birxTninxna dhavxjdalilx (rUDhiyAgi dhavxjsatxMBada magugxlina meVlu mUleyalilx kANuva) okUkxT cihenx. 
\num{11} (koLave \mo vugaLanunx sulBavAgi kUDisalu yA beVpaRDisalu baLasuva) joVDaNe salkaraNe; saMyoVjka. \quad\hyperlink{unionfigure}{\raisebox{-0.15cm}[0pt][0pt]{\pdfimage width 0.5cm height 0.5cm {U_Pictures/union.jpg}}} 
\num{12} (hatitx, linanf, reVSemx yA seNbau, \mo vugaLa) misharx neyegx baTeTx. 
\numi{13} 
\banum
\alnum{a} ogUgxDike; saMyoVjne; saMGaTne; oMdugUDuvudu. 
\alnum{b} ogUgxDida sithxti; saMyukatx sithxti; saMGaTita sithxti. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{14} vaqtitx saMGa; vaqtitxnirataru, kAmiRkaru tamamx aBivaqdithx matutx hitarakaSxNegAgi EpaRDisikoMDa okUkxT. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent 
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} \eng{the Union} 
\banum
\alnum{a} saMyukatx rAjyx, rASaTxrX; 1603ralilx iMgelxMDu matutx sAkxTelxMDugaLa okUkxT. 
\alnum{b} 1801ralilx gerxVTf birxTnf matutx airelxMDugaLa okUkxT. 
\alnum{c} 1707ralilx iMgelxMDina hAgU sAkxTelxMDina pAliRmeMTugaLa okUkxT. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} \eng{union down} (vipatitxna sUcaneyAgi) okUkxT cihenx keLage baruvaMte hArisida bAvuT; talekeLagAgi hArisida bAvuT. 
\enum
\emng

\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\numi{1} 
\banum
\alnum{a} oMdu; Eka; EkAMsha; GaTka; \kanmu\ lekAkxcAradalilx `oMdu' eMbaudAgi gaNisuva biDi matutx pUNR vasutx, vayxkitx, athavA avugaLa yA avara taMDa. 
\alnum{b} EkAMsha; oMdu saMkiVNR aKMDadalilx seVriruva ati cikakxdAda biDi vayxkitxgaLalilx, vasutxgaLalilx yA guMpugaLalilx parxti oMdu: \eng{the family as the unit of society} samAjda GaTka, (EkAMsha)veMdu parigaNisida kuTuMba. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{2} `oMdu' eMba saMKeyx. 
\num{3} (itara motatxgaLanunx nideRVshisalu parxmANavAgi tegedukoLuLxva) EkamAna: \eng{unit of heat} tApada EkamAna. \eng{mass per unit volume} oMdu Gana aLate EkAMshakekx, EkamAnakekx iruva darxvayxrAshi. 
\num{4} (viduyxcaPxkitx \mo vugaLige dara vidhisuvAga gaNisuva) EkamAna. 
\num{5} yUniTf TrxsfTxna atayxMta kaniSaThxvAda SeVru. 
\num{6} (saMkiVNRvAda oMdu yaMtarxracaneyalilx vishiSaTxvAda kelsakAkxgi niyoVjisida, Adare oTuTx yaMtarxda BAgavAda) biDi salkaraNe. 
\num{7} (adaraMteyeV iruva, uLidavugaLoDane hoMdikoLaLxleMdu niyoVjisalAda yA oMdara pUraka BAgagaLalilx oMdAgi racisida) piVThoVpakaraN. 
\num{8} (oMdu saMsethxyalilx) GaTka; visheVSa taMDa; vishiSaTxvAda kelsakekxMdu udedxVshisalAda guMpu yA taMDa. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry

\bentry
\word{unity} 
\pron{yUniTi} 
\gl{\nA}
\expl{(\bava\ \eng{unities}).}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} Ekate; aKMDate. 
\num{2} aikayx; samagarxte; aMgaBAgagaLa meVLanadiMda oMdAgi racitavAgiruvudu: \eng{disturb the unity of the idea} BAvada samagarxtege dhakekxyuMTumADu. 
\num{3} aikayxte; sAMgatayx; sAmaMjsayx; aMgaBAgagaLa ucitavAda parasapxra saMbaMdha yA hoMdike: \eng{the picture lacks unity} I citarxdalilx aikayxte, sAMgatayx illx. 
\num{4} vayxSiTx: aKMDa samagarxvAgiruva saMkiVNR vasutx: \eng{a person regarded as a unity} aKMDa samagarxvAgi pariBAvitanAgiruva vayxkitx. 
\num{5} (\ga) oMdu; Eka. 
\num{6} (vayxkitxgaLu \mo vara naDuvaN) hoMdike; sAmarasayx; omamxnasusx: \eng{dwell together in unity} oMdAgi bALu. 
\num{7} ogagxTuTx; aikamatayx. 
\num{8} (raMgaBUmi) = \eng{\hyperlink{unity pagu(3)}{unity \pagu (3)}.} 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} \eng{at unity with} hoMdikoMDu, aikamatayxdiMda. 
\num{2} \eng{national unity} rASeTxrXYkayx(te); rASiTxrXVya Ekate, aikamatayx. 
\hypertarget{unity pagu(3)}{} 
\num{3} \eng{the dramatic unities (the unities of time, place and action)} nATkiVya aikayxgaLu (kAleYkayx, sathxLeYkayx, kirxyeYkayx); (nATkavanunx ADalu hiDiyuva kAlvU nATkada kathe nijvAgi naDeyalu beVkAda kAlvU sarisumAru oMdeV parimiti uLaLxdAdxgiruvudu kAleYkayx, daqshayx badalAvaNe illxde, oTuTx kathe oMdeV sathxLadalAlxdaMte toVrisuvudu sathxLeYkayx, kathAvasutxvige neVra saMbaMdhavillxdadxnenxlAlx biTuTx katheyanunx omumxKvAgi naDesuvudu kirxyeYkayx). 
\enum
\emng

\bentry
\word[up(1)]{up} 
\pron{apf} 
\gl{\kirxvi}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} meVle; meVlkekx; meVlugaDe (yalilx); meVlugaDege: \eng{high up in the air} (meVle) AkAshadalilx. \eng{what are they doing up there?} alilx meVle avaru Enu mADutitxdAdxre? \eng{lives four floors up} meVle nAlkxneya aMtasitxnalilx vAsisutAtxne. \eng{went up three places in class} avanu taragatiyalilx mUru sAthxna(daSuTx) meVlkekxVrida. 
\num{2} (\AmA) alilx muMdugaDe; alilx meVlugaDe: \eng{went up front} muMdina sAlige hoVda. 
\num{3} (hiMde) yAvudoV kAldavarege. 
\num{4} nadiya meVlkekx, mUldavarege: \eng{follow a stream up to its source} nadiya meVlkekx, mUldavarege (jADu hiDidu) hoVgu. 
\num{5} oLanADinalilx. 
\num{6} (jUjukudureya savArana \vi) kudure Eri, hatitx. 
\num{7} oMdu samathaR yA kAyARtamxkavAda yA parxgatiya sithxtiyalilx yA sithxtige: \eng{stirred up trouble} samaseyx huTuTx hAkida. \eng{the house is up for sale} mane mArATkikxde. \eng{the hunt is up} beVTe yA shoVdhane shuru Agide. 
\num{8} kalitu yA tiLidu: \eng{is well up in French} pherxMcanunx cenAnxgi kalitukoMDidAdxne. 
\num{9} (rasetx \mo vugaLa \vi) ripeVriyalilx; durasitxnalilx. 
\numi{10} 
\banum

\alnum{b} (ATgArana \vi) (hAge inonxMdu taMDa yA ATgAranigiMta) hecucx gellxMka gaLisi. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{11} nAyxyAlya yA nAyxyAdhiVshana muMde hAjrupaDisi: \eng{was brought up for speeding} ati veVgavAgi ODisida kAraNkAkxgi nAyxyAlyada muMde hAjrupaDisalAyitu.

\num{13} (padAthaR \mo vugaLa \vi) bele Eri: \eng{meat is up this week} I vAra mAMsada bele Eride. 
\num{14} (nATkashAleya parade) (raMgasathxLa kANisuvaMte) parade -- meVlkekx Eri, meVledudx. 
\num{15} (mAtanADuvavanu niMtiruva yA sUcisida) sathxLada yA kAldavarege baMdu, samiVpisi: \eng{the child came up and asked me the time} magu nananx baLi baMdu `eSuTx gaMTe' eMdu keVLitu. \eng{went straight up to the door} neVravAgi bAgilvarege hoVda. \eng{has been up till now} iduvarege cenAnxgi, AroVgayxvAgidAdxne. 
\numi{16} 
\banum
\alnum{a} (hAsige \mo vugaLiMda) meVlkekxdudx. 
\alnum{b} (piVThadalilx kuLitavanu, maMDiyUri kuLitavanu) meVledudx niMtu: \eng{sprang up from his seat} avanu piVThadiMda Pakakxne meVledudx niMta. 
\alnum{c} (caTuvaTikeya sUcaneyAgi) meVledudx; meVlkekx ebibxsi (modalAdAdxgi): \eng{put your umbrella up} ninanx Catirx bicicx meVletutx. 
\alnum{d} nililxsi; niMtiruva sithxtiyalilx: \eng{stood it up} adanunx nililxsida. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{17} (\BAavayx dalilx) edudxniMtu; meVlkekx niMtu. 
\num{18} parisharxma paDedu; kalitu; shikaSxNhoMdi: \eng{he is well up in mathematics} avanige gaNitadalilx oLeLxya parisharxmavide.

\num{25} aDakavAda, sheVKrisida yA suBadarxvAda sithxtige taMdu: \eng{pack up} poTTxN kaTuTx. \eng{bind up} kaTuTxgaLanAnxgi mADu. \eng{store up} sheVKra mADu. \eng{lock up} surakiSxtavAgi, BadarxvAgi -- biVga hAki BadarxpaDisu.

\num{31} hAsigeyiMda edudx: \eng{are you up yet?} niVnu inUnx edidxdidxVyA?

\expl{}

\num{4} (loVhada kelsa) moVTu mADu; gujujx mADu; (loVhavanunx, \kanmu\ paTiTxyanunx) eraDu kaDegaLalUlx baDidu yA otitx giDaDxnAgi, dapapxnAgi AguvaMte mADu.

\bentry
\word[urge(1)]{urge} 
\pron{ajfR} 
\gl{\sakirx}
\expl{}
\bmng
\bnum
\num{1} joVrAgi, balAtAkxradiMda -- naDasu, ODisu, dUDu: \eng{urged his horse forward} avana kudureyanunx balvaMtavAgi muMdakekx ODisida. 
\numi{2} (sharxdedhxyiMda, satatavAgi) 
\banum
\alnum{a} pArxthiRsu; moreyiDu; koVru. 
\alnum{b} parxcoVdisu; perxVreVpisu; porxVtAsxhisu: \eng{urged him to action} kAyaRtatapxranAguvaMte parxcoVdisidevu. 
\eanum
\numie
\num{3} (oMdu kAyaRkarxma \mo vanunx keYkoLuLxvaMte) meVliMda meVle otAtxyapaDisu, otitxheVLu, vAdisu: \eng{he urged upon his pupils the importance of hard work} kaSaTxpaTuTx kelsa mADuvudara agatayxvanunx avanu tananx vidAyxthiRgaLige otAtxyapUvaRkavAgi tiLiyaheVLidanu. 
\num{4} (obabxnanunx) beVDi, vAdisi -- otAtxyapaDisu: \eng{the argument was urged in vain} eSuTx otAtxyisi vAda mADidarU adu niSaPxlvAyitu. \eng{the shopkeeper urged me to buy a coat} aMgiyanunx koLuLxvaMte aMgaDiyavanu nananxnunx otAtxyapaDisida. 
\num{5} (kAraN yA samathaRneyAgi) muMdiDu; muMdoDuDx; vAdisu: \eng{he urged the difficulty of getting supplies} sarabarAyi tarisikoLuLxvudu eSuTx dusatxravenunxvudanunx muMdoDiDxda. 
\enum
\emng

\noindent
\gl{\pagu}

\num{4} mAtina riVti: \eng{his very utterance was spell- binding} avana mAtina riVtiyeV moVDihAkitutx. 
\num{5} (\BAshA) shabadxsaMtAna yA padasaMtAna; vAyxkaraNbadadhxvAda yAvudeV oMdu AMshika yA pUNR GaTakavAgirabeVkAgirada, ucacxrita yA liKita padagaLa aviciPxnanx saraNi. 
\enum
\emng
\eentry
